title: "Object Types"
description: "All object types in the GraphQL schema"
noindex: true

## AddEventsByMakerOutput

Response returned by `onEventsCreatedByMaker`.

<ResponseField name="makerAddress" type="String!" required>
  The address of the maker.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="events" type="[Event!]!" required>
  A list of transactions for the maker.
</ResponseField>

```graphql 
"""Response returned by `onEventsCreatedByMaker`."""
type AddEventsByMakerOutput {
  """The address of the maker."""
  makerAddress: String!
  """A list of transactions for the maker."""
  events: [Event!]!
}
```

---

## AddEventsOutput

Response returned by `onEventsCreated`.

<ResponseField name="address" type="String!" required>
  The contract address of the pair.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="networkId" type="Int!" required>
  The network ID that the token is deployed on.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="id" type="String!" required>
  The ID of the event (`address`:`networkId`). For example, `0xc02aaa39b223fe8d0a0e5c4f27ead9083c756cc2:1`.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="quoteToken" type="QuoteToken">
  The token of interest within the pair. Can be `token0` or `token1`.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="events" type="[Event]!" required>
  A list of transactions for the token.
</ResponseField>

```graphql 
"""Response returned by `onEventsCreated`."""
type AddEventsOutput {
  """The contract address of the pair."""
  address: String!
  """The network ID that the token is deployed on."""
  networkId: Int!
  """The ID of the event (`address`:`networkId`). For example, `0xc02aaa39b223fe8d0a0e5c4f27ead9083c756cc2:1`."""
  id: String!
  """The token of interest within the pair. Can be `token0` or `token1`."""
  quoteToken: QuoteToken
  """A list of transactions for the token."""
  events: [Event]!
}
```

---

## AddNftEventsOutput

Response returned by `onNftEventsCreated`.

<ResponseField name="address" type="String!" required>
  The contract address of the NFT collection.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="networkId" type="Int!" required>
  The network ID the collection is deployed on.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="id" type="String!" required>
  The id of the collection (`address`:`networkId`).
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="events" type="[NftEvent]!" required>
  A list of NFT transactions streaming real-time.
</ResponseField>

```graphql 
"""Response returned by `onNftEventsCreated`."""
type AddNftEventsOutput {
  """The contract address of the NFT collection."""
  address: String!
  """The network ID the collection is deployed on."""
  networkId: Int!
  """The id of the collection (`address`:`networkId`)."""
  id: String!
  """A list of NFT transactions streaming real-time."""
  events: [NftEvent]!
}
```

## AddUnconfirmedEventsOutput

Response returned by `onUnconfirmedEventsCreated`.

<ResponseField name="address" type="String!" required>
  The contract address of the pair.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="networkId" type="Int!" required>
  The network ID that the token is deployed on.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="id" type="String!" required>
  The ID of the event (`address`:`networkId`). For example, `0xc02aaa39b223fe8d0a0e5c4f27ead9083c756cc2:1`.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="quoteToken" type="QuoteToken">
  The token of interest within the pair. Can be `token0` or `token1`.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="events" type="[UnconfirmedEvent]!" required>
  A list of transactions for the token.
</ResponseField>

```graphql 
"""Response returned by `onUnconfirmedEventsCreated`."""
type AddUnconfirmedEventsOutput {
  """The contract address of the pair."""
  address: String!
  """The network ID that the token is deployed on."""
  networkId: Int!
  """The ID of the event (`address`:`networkId`). For example, `0xc02aaa39b223fe8d0a0e5c4f27ead9083c756cc2:1`."""
  id: String!
  """The token of interest within the pair. Can be `token0` or `token1`."""
  quoteToken: QuoteToken
  """A list of transactions for the token."""
  events: [UnconfirmedEvent]!
}
```

## ApiToken

<ResponseField name="id" type="String!" required>
  Unique identifier for the token
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="token" type="String!" required>
  JWT to be passed into the Authorization header for API requests
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="expiresTimeString" type="String!" required>
  ISO time string for the expiry of the token
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="requestLimit" type="String!" required>
  Number of root fields this api token is allowed to resolve before it's rate limited
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="remaining" type="String">
  Approximate number of remaining resolutions before this token is rate limited
</ResponseField>

```graphql 
type ApiToken {
  """Unique identifier for the token"""
  id: String!
  """JWT to be passed into the Authorization header for API requests"""
  token: String!
  """ISO time string for the expiry of the token"""
  expiresTimeString: String!
  """Number of root fields this api token is allowed to resolve before it's rate limited"""
  requestLimit: String!
  """Approximate number of remaining resolutions before this token is rate limited"""
  remaining: String
}
```

---

## Balance

Wallet balance of a token.

<ResponseField name="walletId" type="String!" required>
  The ID of the wallet (`walletAddress:networkId`).
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="tokenId" type="String!" required>
  The ID of the token (`tokenAddress:networkId`).
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="address" type="String!" required>
  The wallet address.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="networkId" type="Int!" required>
  The wallet network.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="tokenAddress" type="String!" required>
  The contract address of the token.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="balance" type="String!" required>
  The balance held by the wallet.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="shiftedBalance" type="Float!" required>
  The balance held by the wallet, adjusted by the number of decimals in the token.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="balanceUsd" type="String">
  The balance held by the wallet in USD.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="tokenPriceUsd" type="String">
  The token price in USD.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="firstHeldTimestamp" type="Int">
  The time that this address first held a token.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="token" type="EnhancedToken">
  Metadata for the token.
</ResponseField>

```graphql 
"""Wallet balance of a token."""
type Balance {
  """The ID of the wallet (`walletAddress:networkId`)."""
  walletId: String!
  """The ID of the token (`tokenAddress:networkId`)."""
  tokenId: String!
  """The wallet address."""
  address: String!
  """The wallet network."""
  networkId: Int!
  """The contract address of the token."""
  tokenAddress: String!
  """The balance held by the wallet."""
  balance: String!
  """The balance held by the wallet, adjusted by the number of decimals in the token."""
  shiftedBalance: Float!
  """The balance held by the wallet in USD."""
  balanceUsd: String
  """The token price in USD."""
  tokenPriceUsd: String
  """The time that this address first held a token."""
  firstHeldTimestamp: Int
  """Metadata for the token."""
  token: EnhancedToken
}
```

---

## BalancesResponse

<ResponseField name="items" type="[Balance!]!" required>
  The list of token balances that a wallet has.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="cursor" type="String">
  A cursor for use in pagination.
</ResponseField>

```graphql 
type BalancesResponse {
  """The list of token balances that a wallet has."""
  items: [Balance!]!
  """A cursor for use in pagination."""
  cursor: String
}
```

## BarsResponse

Bar chart data to track price changes over time.

<ResponseField name="o" type="[Float]!" required>
  The opening price.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="h" type="[Float]!" required>
  The high price.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="l" type="[Float]!" required>
  The low price.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="c" type="[Float]!" required>
  The closing price.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="v" type="[Int]!" required>
  The volume.
  
  <Warning>
    This field is deprecated. Use volume field instead
  </Warning>
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="t" type="[Int!]!" required>
  The timestamp for the bar.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="s" type="String!" required>
  The status code for the batch: `ok` for successful data retrieval and `no_data` for empty responses signaling the end of server data.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="volume" type="[String]">
  The volume with higher precision.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="volumeNativeToken" type="[String]">
  The volume in the native token for the network
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="buyers" type="[Int]!" required>
  The number of unique buyers
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="buys" type="[Int]!" required>
  The number of buys
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="buyVolume" type="[String]!" required>
  The buy volume in USD
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="sellers" type="[Int]!" required>
  The number of unique sellers
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="sells" type="[Int]!" required>
  The number of sells
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="sellVolume" type="[String]!" required>
  The sell volume in USD
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="liquidity" type="[String]!" required>
  Liquidity in USD
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="traders" type="[Int]!" required>
  The number of traders
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="transactions" type="[Int]!" required>
  The number of transactions
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="pair" type="Pair!" required>
  The pair that is being returned
</ResponseField>

```graphql 
"""Bar chart data to track price changes over time."""
type BarsResponse {
  """The opening price."""
  o: [Float]!
  """The high price."""
  h: [Float]!
  """The low price."""
  l: [Float]!
  """The closing price."""
  c: [Float]!
  """The volume."""
  v: [Int]! @deprecated(reason: "Use volume field instead")
  """The timestamp for the bar."""
  t: [Int!]!
  """The status code for the batch: `ok` for successful data retrieval and `no_data` for empty responses signaling the end of server data."""
  s: String!
  """The volume with higher precision."""
  volume: [String]
  """The volume in the native token for the network"""
  volumeNativeToken: [String]
  """The number of unique buyers"""
  buyers: [Int]!
  """The number of buys"""
  buys: [Int]!
  """The buy volume in USD"""
  buyVolume: [String]!
  """The number of unique sellers"""
  sellers: [Int]!
  """The number of sells"""
  sells: [Int]!
  """The sell volume in USD"""
  sellVolume: [String]!
  """Liquidity in USD"""
  liquidity: [String]!
  """The number of traders"""
  traders: [Int]!
  """The number of transactions"""
  transactions: [Int]!
  """The pair that is being returned"""
  pair: Pair!
}
```

---

## BurnEventData

Event data for a token burn event.

<ResponseField name="amount0" type="String">
  The amount of `token0` removed from the pair.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="amount1" type="String">
  The amount of `token1` removed from the pair.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="amount0Shifted" type="String">
  The amount of `token0` removed from the pair, adjusted by the number of decimals in the token. For example, if `amount0` is in WEI, `amount0Shifted` will be in ETH.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="amount1Shifted" type="String">
  The amount of `token1` removed from the pair, adjusted by the number of decimals in the token. For example, USDC `amount1Shifted` will be by 6 decimals.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="tickLower" type="String">
  The lower tick boundary of the position. Only applicable for UniswapV3 events.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="tickUpper" type="String">
  The upper tick boundary of the position. Only applicable for UniswapV3 events.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="type" type="EventType!" required>
  The type of token event, `Burn`.
</ResponseField>

```graphql 
"""Event data for a token burn event."""
type BurnEventData {
  """The amount of `token0` removed from the pair."""
  amount0: String
  """The amount of `token1` removed from the pair."""
  amount1: String
  """The amount of `token0` removed from the pair, adjusted by the number of decimals in the token. For example, if `amount0` is in WEI, `amount0Shifted` will be in ETH."""
  amount0Shifted: String
  """The amount of `token1` removed from the pair, adjusted by the number of decimals in the token. For example, USDC `amount1Shifted` will be by 6 decimals."""
  amount1Shifted: String
  """The lower tick boundary of the position. Only applicable for UniswapV3 events."""
  tickLower: String
  """The upper tick boundary of the position. Only applicable for UniswapV3 events."""
  tickUpper: String
  """The type of token event, `Burn`."""
  type: EventType!
}
```

---

## CommunityNote

Community gathered proposals for an asset.

<ResponseField name="address" type="String!" required>
  The contract address of the contract.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="contractType" type="ContractType!" required>
  No description provided
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="currentContract" type="EnhancedContract">
  No description provided
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="currentData" type="JSON">
  The contract after the community note was applied.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="id" type="String!" required>
  The ID of the contract (`address:id`).
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="moderatedAt" type="Int">
  The unix timestamp of when the community note was moderated.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="networkId" type="Int!" required>
  The network ID the contract is deployed on.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="previousData" type="JSON">
  The contract before the community note was applied.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="proposalData" type="JSON!" required>
  The data of the community note.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="proposalNum" type="Int!" required>
  The ordinal number of the community note.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="proposalType" type="CommunityNoteType!" required>
  The type of the community note.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="proposedAt" type="Int!" required>
  The unix timestamp of when the community note was created.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="status" type="ContractProposalStatus!" required>
  The status of the community note.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="sortKey" type="String!" required>
  No description provided
</ResponseField>

```graphql 
"""Community gathered proposals for an asset."""
type CommunityNote {
  """The contract address of the contract."""
  address: String!
  contractType: ContractType!
  currentContract: EnhancedContract
  """The contract after the community note was applied."""
  currentData: JSON
  """The ID of the contract (`address:id`)."""
  id: String!
  """The unix timestamp of when the community note was moderated."""
  moderatedAt: Int
  """The network ID the contract is deployed on."""
  networkId: Int!
  """The contract before the community note was applied."""
  previousData: JSON
  """The data of the community note."""
  proposalData: JSON!
  """The ordinal number of the community note."""
  proposalNum: Int!
  """The type of the community note."""
  proposalType: CommunityNoteType!
  """The unix timestamp of when the community note was created."""
  proposedAt: Int!
  """The status of the community note."""
  status: ContractProposalStatus!
  sortKey: String!
}
```

## ComparisonOperator

Comparison operators.

<ResponseField name="gt" type="String">
  Greater than.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="gte" type="String">
  Greater than or equal to.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="lt" type="String">
  Less than.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="lte" type="String">
  Less than or equal to.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="eq" type="String">
  Equal to.
</ResponseField>

```graphql 
"""Comparison operators."""
type ComparisonOperator {
  """Greater than."""
  gt: String
  """Greater than or equal to."""
  gte: String
  """Less than."""
  lt: String
  """Less than or equal to."""
  lte: String
  """Equal to."""
  eq: String
}
```

## ContractLabel

Metadata for a contract label.

<ResponseField name="createdAt" type="Int!" required>
  The unix timestamp for when the contract label was created.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="subType" type="ContractLabelSubType!" required>
  The contract label sub-type. Can be `Generic`, `HighTax`, `HoneyPot` or `Imitator`.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="type" type="ContractLabelType!" required>
  The contract label type. Can be `Scam`.
</ResponseField>

```graphql 
"""Metadata for a contract label."""
type ContractLabel {
  """The unix timestamp for when the contract label was created."""
  createdAt: Int!
  """The contract label sub-type. Can be `Generic`, `HighTax`, `HoneyPot` or `Imitator`."""
  subType: ContractLabelSubType!
  """The contract label type. Can be `Scam`."""
  type: ContractLabelType!
}
```

</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="nftEventWebhooks" type="[Webhook]!" required>
  The list of NFT event webhooks that were created.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="rawTransactionWebhooks" type="[Webhook]!" required>
  The list of raw transaction webhooks that were created.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="marketCapWebhooks" type="[Webhook]!" required>
  The list of market cap event webhooks that were created.
</ResponseField>

```graphql 
"""Result returned by `createWebhooks`."""
type CreateWebhooksOutput {
  """The list of price webhooks that were created."""
  priceWebhooks: [Webhook]!
  """The list of token pair event webhooks that were created."""
  tokenPairEventWebhooks: [Webhook]!
  """The list of NFT event webhooks that were created."""
  nftEventWebhooks: [Webhook]!
  """The list of raw transaction webhooks that were created."""
  rawTransactionWebhooks: [Webhook]!
  """The list of market cap event webhooks that were created."""
  marketCapWebhooks: [Webhook]!
}
```

</ResponseField>

  Bar chart data in the network's base token.
</ResponseField>

```graphql

type CurrencyBarData {
  """The timestamp for the bar."""
  t: Int!
  """Bar chart data in USD."""
  usd: IndividualBarData!
  """Bar chart data in the network's base token."""
  token: IndividualBarData!
}
```

## DetailedNftStats

Detailed stats for an NFT collection.

<ResponseField name="collectionAddress" type="String!" required>
  The contract address of the NFT collection.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="networkId" type="Int!" required>
  The network ID the NFT collection is deployed on.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="grouping" type="String">
  The marketplace address or `all`. Can be used to get marketplace-specific metrics.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="stats_hour1" type="WindowedDetailedNftStats">
  The breakdown of stats over an hour window.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="stats_hour4" type="WindowedDetailedNftStats">
  The breakdown of stats over a 4 hour window.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="stats_hour12" type="WindowedDetailedNftStats">
  The breakdown of stats over a 12 hour window.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="stats_day1" type="WindowedDetailedNftStats">
  The breakdown of stats over a 24 hour window.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="stats_week1" type="WindowedDetailedNftStats">
  The breakdown of stats over a 7 day window.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="stats_day30" type="WindowedDetailedNftStats">
  The breakdown of stats over a 30 day window.
</ResponseField>

```graphql 
"""Detailed stats for an NFT collection."""
type DetailedNftStats {
  """The contract address of the NFT collection."""
  collectionAddress: String!
  """The network ID the NFT collection is deployed on."""
  networkId: Int!
  """The marketplace address or `all`. Can be used to get marketplace-specific metrics."""
  grouping: String
  """The breakdown of stats over an hour window."""
  stats_hour1: WindowedDetailedNftStats
  """The breakdown of stats over a 4 hour window."""
  stats_hour4: WindowedDetailedNftStats
  """The breakdown of stats over a 12 hour window."""
  stats_hour12: WindowedDetailedNftStats
  """The breakdown of stats over a 24 hour window."""
  stats_day1: WindowedDetailedNftStats
  """The breakdown of stats over a 7 day window."""
  stats_week1: WindowedDetailedNftStats
  """The breakdown of stats over a 30 day window."""
  stats_day30: WindowedDetailedNftStats
}
```

---

## DetailedNftStatsBucketTimestamp

The start/end timestamp for a given bucket within the window.

  The unix timestamp for the end of the window.
</ResponseField>

```graphql 
  """The unix timestamp for the start of the window."""

  """The unix timestamp for the end of the window."""
  end: Int!
}
```

</ResponseField>

</ResponseField>

## DetailedPairStats

Detailed stats for a token within a pair.

<ResponseField name="pairAddress" type="String!" required>
  The contract address of the pair.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="networkId" type="Int!" required>
  The network ID the pair is deployed on.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="tokenOfInterest" type="TokenOfInterest">
  The token of interest used to calculate token-specific stats.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="lastTransaction" type="Int">
  The unix timestamp for the last transaction to happen on the pair.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="statsType" type="TokenPairStatisticsType!" required>
  The type of statistics returned. Can be `FILTERED` or `UNFILTERED`
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="stats_min5" type="WindowedDetailedPairStats">
  The breakdown of stats over a 5 minute window.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="stats_min15" type="WindowedDetailedPairStats">
  The breakdown of stats over a 15 minute window.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="stats_hour1" type="WindowedDetailedPairStats">
  The breakdown of stats over an hour window.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="stats_hour4" type="WindowedDetailedPairStats">
  The breakdown of stats over a 4 hour window.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="stats_hour12" type="WindowedDetailedPairStats">
  The breakdown of stats over a 12 hour window.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="stats_day1" type="WindowedDetailedPairStats">
  The breakdown of stats over a 24 hour window.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="stats_week1" type="WindowedDetailedPairStats">
  The breakdown of stats over a 7 day window.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="stats_day30" type="WindowedDetailedPairStats">
  The breakdown of stats over a 30 day window.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="bucketCount" type="Int">
  Number of aggregated buckets specified in input
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="queryTimestamp" type="Int">
  The timestamp specified as input to the query
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="pair" type="Pair">
  No description provided
</ResponseField>

```graphql 
"""Detailed stats for a token within a pair."""
type DetailedPairStats {
  """The contract address of the pair."""
  pairAddress: String!
  """The network ID the pair is deployed on."""
  networkId: Int!
  """The token of interest used to calculate token-specific stats."""
  tokenOfInterest: TokenOfInterest
  """The unix timestamp for the last transaction to happen on the pair."""
  lastTransaction: Int
  """The type of statistics returned. Can be `FILTERED` or `UNFILTERED`"""
  statsType: TokenPairStatisticsType!
  """The breakdown of stats over a 5 minute window."""
  stats_min5: WindowedDetailedPairStats
  """The breakdown of stats over a 15 minute window."""
  stats_min15: WindowedDetailedPairStats
  """The breakdown of stats over an hour window."""
  stats_hour1: WindowedDetailedPairStats
  """The breakdown of stats over a 4 hour window."""
  stats_hour4: WindowedDetailedPairStats
  """The breakdown of stats over a 12 hour window."""
  stats_hour12: WindowedDetailedPairStats
  """The breakdown of stats over a 24 hour window."""
  stats_day1: WindowedDetailedPairStats
  """The breakdown of stats over a 7 day window."""
  stats_week1: WindowedDetailedPairStats
  """The breakdown of stats over a 30 day window."""
  stats_day30: WindowedDetailedPairStats
  """Number of aggregated buckets specified in input"""
  bucketCount: Int
  """The timestamp specified as input to the query"""
  queryTimestamp: Int
  pair: Pair
}
```

## DetailedStats

<ResponseField name="pairId" type="String!" required>

</ResponseField>

</ResponseField>

</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="stats_min5" type="WindowedDetailedStats">
  The breakdown of stats over a 5 minute window.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="stats_hour1" type="WindowedDetailedStats">
  The breakdown of stats over an hour window.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="stats_hour4" type="WindowedDetailedStats">
  The breakdown of stats over a 4 hour window.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="stats_hour12" type="WindowedDetailedStats">
  The breakdown of stats over a 12 hour window.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="stats_day1" type="WindowedDetailedStats">
  The breakdown of stats over a 24 hour window.
</ResponseField>

</ResponseField>

## DetailedWalletStats

The detailed stats for a wallet.

<ResponseField name="walletAddress" type="String!" required>
  The wallet address
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="lastTransactionAt" type="Int!" required>
  The last transaction timestamp
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="networkSpecificStats" type="[NetworkWalletStats!]">
  The network specific stats
  
  <Warning>
    This field is deprecated. Use networkBreakdown instead
  </Warning>
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="networkBreakdown" type="[NetworkBreakdown!]">
  The network breakdown
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="labels" type="[String!]!" required>
  The labels associated with the wallet
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="scammerScore" type="Int">
  The likelihood of the wallet being a scammer
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="botScore" type="Int">
  The likelihood of the wallet being a bot
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="statsDay1" type="WindowedWalletStats">
  The stats for the last day
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="statsWeek1" type="WindowedWalletStats">
  The stats for the last week
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="statsDay30" type="WindowedWalletStats">
  The stats for the last 30 days
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="statsYear1" type="WindowedWalletStats">
  The stats for the last year
</ResponseField>

```graphql 
"""The detailed stats for a wallet."""
type DetailedWalletStats {
  """The wallet address"""
  walletAddress: String!
  """The last transaction timestamp"""
  lastTransactionAt: Int!
  """The network specific stats"""
  networkSpecificStats: [NetworkWalletStats!] @deprecated(reason: "Use networkBreakdown instead")
  """The network breakdown"""
  networkBreakdown: [NetworkBreakdown!]
  """The labels associated with the wallet"""
  labels: [String!]!
  """The likelihood of the wallet being a scammer"""
  scammerScore: Int
  """The likelihood of the wallet being a bot"""
  botScore: Int
  """The stats for the last day"""
  statsDay1: WindowedWalletStats
  """The stats for the last week"""
  statsWeek1: WindowedWalletStats
  """The stats for the last 30 days"""
  statsDay30: WindowedWalletStats
  """The stats for the last year"""
  statsYear1: WindowedWalletStats
}
```

## EnhancedNftContract

Metadata for an NFT collection.

<ResponseField name="id" type="String!" required>
  The ID of the NFT collection (`address`:`networkId`).
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="address" type="String!" required>
  The contract address of the NFT collection.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="networkId" type="Int!" required>
  The network ID the NFT collection is deployed on.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="ercType" type="String!" required>
  The token standard. Can be a variation of `ERC-721` or `ERC-1155`.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="name" type="String">
  The name of the NFT collection.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="description" type="String">
  The description of the NFT collection.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="symbol" type="String">
  The symbol of the NFT collection.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="totalSupply" type="String">
  The total supply of the NFT collection.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="socialLinks" type="SocialLinks">
  Community gathered links for the socials of this NFT collection.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="image" type="String">
  The URL for an image of the NFT collection.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="labels" type="[ContractLabel]">
  A list of labels for the NFT collection.
</ResponseField>

```graphql 
"""Metadata for an NFT collection."""
type EnhancedNftContract {
  """The ID of the NFT collection (`address`:`networkId`)."""
  id: String!
  """The contract address of the NFT collection."""
  address: String!
  """The network ID the NFT collection is deployed on."""
  networkId: Int!
  """The token standard. Can be a variation of `ERC-721` or `ERC-1155`."""
  ercType: String!
  """The name of the NFT collection."""
  name: String
  """The description of the NFT collection."""
  description: String
  """The symbol of the NFT collection."""
  symbol: String
  """The total supply of the NFT collection."""
  totalSupply: String
  """Community gathered links for the socials of this NFT collection."""
  socialLinks: SocialLinks
  """The URL for an image of the NFT collection."""
  image: String
  """A list of labels for the NFT collection."""
  labels: [ContractLabel]
}
```

## EnhancedToken

Metadata for a token.

<ResponseField name="address" type="String!" required>
  The contract address of the token.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="cmcId" type="Int">
  The token ID on CoinMarketCap.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="decimals" type="Int!" required>
  The precision to which the token can be divided. For example, the smallest unit for USDC is 0.000001 (6 decimals).
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="id" type="String!" required>
  The ID of the token (`address:networkId`).
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="isScam" type="Boolean">
  Whether the token has been flagged as a scam.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="name" type="String">
  The token name. For example, `ApeCoin`.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="networkId" type="Int!" required>
  The network ID the token is deployed on.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="symbol" type="String">
  The token symbol. For example, `APE`.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="totalSupply" type="String">
  The total supply of the token.
  
  <Warning>
    This field is deprecated. Use the TokenInfo type
  </Warning>
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="socialLinks" type="SocialLinks">
  Community gathered links for the socials of this token.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="info" type="TokenInfo">
  More metadata about the token.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="explorerData" type="ExplorerTokenData">
  Information about the token from 3rd party sources.
  
  <Warning>
    This field is deprecated. Use the TokenInfo type
  </Warning>
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="exchanges" type="[Exchange!]">
  A list of exchanges where the token has been traded.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="imageThumbUrl" type="String">
  The thumbnail token logo URL.
  
  <Warning>
    This field is deprecated. Use the TokenInfo type
  </Warning>
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="imageSmallUrl" type="String">
  The small token logo URL.
  
  <Warning>
    This field is deprecated. Use the TokenInfo type
  </Warning>
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="imageLargeUrl" type="String">
  The large token logo URL.
  
  <Warning>
    This field is deprecated. Use the TokenInfo type
  </Warning>
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="circulatingSupply" type="String">
  The circulating supply of the token.
  
  <Warning>
    This field is deprecated. Use the TokenInfo type
  </Warning>
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="pooled" type="String">
  The amount of this token in the pair.
  
  <Warning>
    This field is deprecated. Pooled can be found on the pair instead
  </Warning>
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="creatorAddress" type="String">
  The token creator's wallet address.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="createBlockNumber" type="Int">
  The block height the token was created at.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="createTransactionHash" type="String">
  The transaction hash of the token's creation.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="createdAt" type="Int">
  The unix timestamp for the creation of the token.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="mintable" type="String">
  Whether or not the token is mintable
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="freezable" type="String">
  Whether or not the token is freezable
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="launchpad" type="LaunchpadData">
  The launchpad data for the token, if applicable.
</ResponseField>

```graphql 
"""Metadata for a token."""
type EnhancedToken {
  """The contract address of the token."""
  address: String!
  """The token ID on CoinMarketCap."""
  cmcId: Int
  """The precision to which the token can be divided. For example, the smallest unit for USDC is 0.000001 (6 decimals)."""
  decimals: Int!
  """The ID of the token (`address:networkId`)."""
  id: String!
  """Whether the token has been flagged as a scam."""
  isScam: Boolean
  """The token name. For example, `ApeCoin`."""
  name: String
  """The network ID the token is deployed on."""
  networkId: Int!
  """The token symbol. For example, `APE`."""
  symbol: String
  """The total supply of the token."""
  totalSupply: String @deprecated(reason: "Use the TokenInfo type")
  """Community gathered links for the socials of this token."""
  socialLinks: SocialLinks
  """More metadata about the token."""
  info: TokenInfo
  """Information about the token from 3rd party sources."""
  explorerData: ExplorerTokenData @deprecated(reason: "Use the TokenInfo type")
  """A list of exchanges where the token has been traded."""
  exchanges: [Exchange!]
  """The thumbnail token logo URL."""
  imageThumbUrl: String @deprecated(reason: "Use the TokenInfo type")
  """The small token logo URL."""
  imageSmallUrl: String @deprecated(reason: "Use the TokenInfo type")
  """The large token logo URL."""
  imageLargeUrl: String @deprecated(reason: "Use the TokenInfo type")
  """The circulating supply of the token."""
  circulatingSupply: String @deprecated(reason: "Use the TokenInfo type")
  """The amount of this token in the pair."""
  pooled: String @deprecated(reason: "Pooled can be found on the pair instead")
  """The token creator's wallet address."""
  creatorAddress: String
  """The block height the token was created at."""
  createBlockNumber: Int
  """The transaction hash of the token's creation."""
  createTransactionHash: String
  """The unix timestamp for the creation of the token."""
  createdAt: Int
  """Whether or not the token is mintable"""
  mintable: String
  """Whether or not the token is freezable"""
  freezable: String
  """The launchpad data for the token, if applicable."""
  launchpad: LaunchpadData
}
```

---

## Event

A token transaction.

<ResponseField name="address" type="String!" required>
  The contract address of the token's top pair.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="baseTokenPrice" type="String">
  The price of the network's base token.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="blockHash" type="String!" required>
  The hash of the block where the transaction occurred.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="blockNumber" type="Int!" required>
  The block number for the transaction.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="data" type="EventData">
  The event-specific data for the transaction. Can be `BurnEventData` or `MintEventData` or `SwapEventData`.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="eventType" type="EventType!" required>
  The type of transaction event. Can be `Burn`, `Mint`, `Swap`, `Sync`, `Collect`, or `CollectProtocol`.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="id" type="String!" required>
  The ID of the event (`address:networkId`). For example, `0xc02aaa39b223fe8d0a0e5c4f27ead9083c756cc2:1`.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="liquidityToken" type="String">
  The contract address of the token with higher liquidity in the token's top pair.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="logIndex" type="Int!" required>
  The index of the log in the block.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="maker" type="String">
  The wallet address that performed the transaction.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="networkId" type="Int!" required>
  The network ID that the token is deployed on.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="quoteToken" type="QuoteToken">
  The token of interest within the token's top pair. Can be `token0` or `token1`.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="timestamp" type="Int!" required>
  The unix timestamp for when the transaction occurred.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="token0Address" type="String">
  The address of the event's token0.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="token1Address" type="String">
  The address of the event's token1.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="token0SwapValueUsd" type="String">
  The price of `token0` paid/received in USD, including any fees.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="token1SwapValueUsd" type="String">
  The price of `token1` paid/received in USD, including any fees.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="token0ValueBase" type="String">
  The price of `token0` paid/received in the network's base token, including fees.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="token1ValueBase" type="String">
  The price of `token1` paid/received in the network's base token, including fees.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="token0PoolValueUsd" type="String">
  The updated price of `token0` in USD, calculated after the transaction.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="token1PoolValueUsd" type="String">
  The updated price of `token1` in USD, calculated after the transaction.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="transactionHash" type="String!" required>
  The unique hash for the transaction.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="transactionIndex" type="Int!" required>
  The index of the transaction within the block.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="eventDisplayType" type="EventDisplayType">
  A more specific breakdown of `eventType`. Splits `Swap` into `Buy` or `Sell`.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="labels" type="LabelsForEvent">
  Labels attributed to the event.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="walletAge" type="Int">
  The age of the wallet in seconds.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="walletLabels" type="[String!]">
  Labels attributed to the wallet.
</ResponseField>

```graphql 
"""A token transaction."""
type Event {
  """The contract address of the token's top pair."""
  address: String!
  """The price of the network's base token."""
  baseTokenPrice: String
  """The hash of the block where the transaction occurred."""
  blockHash: String!
  """The block number for the transaction."""
  blockNumber: Int!
  """The event-specific data for the transaction. Can be `BurnEventData` or `MintEventData` or `SwapEventData`."""
  data: EventData
  """The type of transaction event. Can be `Burn`, `Mint`, `Swap`, `Sync`, `Collect`, or `CollectProtocol`."""
  eventType: EventType!
  """The ID of the event (`address:networkId`). For example, `0xc02aaa39b223fe8d0a0e5c4f27ead9083c756cc2:1`."""
  id: String!
  """The contract address of the token with higher liquidity in the token's top pair."""
  liquidityToken: String
  """The index of the log in the block."""
  logIndex: Int!
  """The wallet address that performed the transaction."""
  maker: String
  """The network ID that the token is deployed on."""
  networkId: Int!
  """The token of interest within the token's top pair. Can be `token0` or `token1`."""
  quoteToken: QuoteToken
  """The unix timestamp for when the transaction occurred."""
  timestamp: Int!
  """The address of the event's token0."""
  token0Address: String
  """The address of the event's token1."""
  token1Address: String
  """The price of `token0` paid/received in USD, including any fees."""
  token0SwapValueUsd: String
  """The price of `token1` paid/received in USD, including any fees."""
  token1SwapValueUsd: String
  """The price of `token0` paid/received in the network's base token, including fees."""
  token0ValueBase: String
  """The price of `token1` paid/received in the network's base token, including fees."""
  token1ValueBase: String
  """The updated price of `token0` in USD, calculated after the transaction."""
  token0PoolValueUsd: String
  """The updated price of `token1` in USD, calculated after the transaction."""
  token1PoolValueUsd: String
  """The unique hash for the transaction."""
  transactionHash: String!
  """The index of the transaction within the block."""
  transactionIndex: Int!
  """A more specific breakdown of `eventType`. Splits `Swap` into `Buy` or `Sell`."""
  eventDisplayType: EventDisplayType
  """Labels attributed to the event."""
  labels: LabelsForEvent
  """The age of the wallet in seconds."""
  walletAge: Int
  """Labels attributed to the wallet."""
  walletLabels: [String!]
}
```

## LatestPair

Metadata for a newly listed pair.

<ResponseField name="address" type="String!" required>
  The contract address for the pair.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="exchangeHash" type="String!" required>
  The contract address for the exchange.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="id" type="String!" required>
  The ID of the pair (`address:networkId`).
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="initialPriceUsd" type="String!" required>
  The listing price, or first known price for the pair, in USD.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="liquidAt" type="Int">
  The unix timestamp for when liquidity was added to the pair.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="liquidity" type="String!" required>
  The total liquidity in the pair.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="liquidityToken" type="String">
  The token with higher liquidity within the pair. Can be `token0` or `token1`.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="networkId" type="Int!" required>
  The network ID the pair is deployed on.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="newToken" type="String!" required>
  The newly added token within the pair. Can be `token0` or `token1`.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="nonLiquidityToken" type="String">
  The token with lower liquidity within the pair. Can be `token0` or `token1`.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="oldToken" type="String!" required>
  The pre-existing token within the pair. Can be `token0` or `token1`.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="priceChange" type="Float!" required>
  The percent price change between the listing price and the current price.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="priceUsd" type="String!" required>
  The newly added token price in USD.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="token0" type="LatestPairToken!" required>
  Metadata for `token0`.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="token1" type="LatestPairToken!" required>
  Metadata for `token1`.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="transactionHash" type="String!" required>
  The unique hash for the transaction that added liquidity, if applicable, otherwise the transaction that added the pair.
</ResponseField>

```graphql 
"""Metadata for a newly listed pair."""
type LatestPair {
  """The contract address for the pair."""
  address: String!
  """The contract address for the exchange."""
  exchangeHash: String!
  """The ID of the pair (`address:networkId`)."""
  id: String!
  """The listing price, or first known price for the pair, in USD."""
  initialPriceUsd: String!
  """The unix timestamp for when liquidity was added to the pair."""
  liquidAt: Int
  """The total liquidity in the pair."""
  liquidity: String!
  """The token with higher liquidity within the pair. Can be `token0` or `token1`."""
  liquidityToken: String
  """The network ID the pair is deployed on."""
  networkId: Int!
  """The newly added token within the pair. Can be `token0` or `token1`."""
  newToken: String!
  """The token with lower liquidity within the pair. Can be `token0` or `token1`."""
  nonLiquidityToken: String
  """The pre-existing token within the pair. Can be `token0` or `token1`."""
  oldToken: String!
  """The percent price change between the listing price and the current price."""
  priceChange: Float!
  """The newly added token price in USD."""
  priceUsd: String!
  """Metadata for `token0`."""
  token0: LatestPairToken!
  """Metadata for `token1`."""
  token1: LatestPairToken!
  """The unique hash for the transaction that added liquidity, if applicable, otherwise the transaction that added the pair."""
  transactionHash: String!
}
```

---

## LatestPairToken

<ResponseField name="address" type="String!" required>
  The contract address for the token.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="currentPoolAmount" type="String!" required>
  The amount of `token` currently in the pair.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="decimals" type="Int!" required>
  The precision to which the token can be divided. For example, the smallest unit for USDC is 0.000001 (6 decimals).
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="id" type="String!" required>
  The ID of the token (`address:networkId`).
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="initialPoolAmount" type="String!" required>
  The initial amount of `token` added to the pair.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="name" type="String!" required>
  The name of the token.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="networkId" type="Int!" required>
  The network ID the token is deployed on.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="pairId" type="String!" required>
  The ID of the pair (`pairAddress:networkId`).
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="poolVariation" type="Float!" required>
  The percent change `token` remaining in the pair since the initial add.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="symbol" type="String!" required>
  The symbol for the token.
</ResponseField>

```graphql 
"""Metadata for a token within a newly listed pair."""
type LatestPairToken {
  """The contract address for the token."""
  address: String!
  """The amount of `token` currently in the pair."""
  currentPoolAmount: String!
  """The precision to which the token can be divided. For example, the smallest unit for USDC is 0.000001 (6 decimals)."""
  decimals: Int!
  """The ID of the token (`address:networkId`)."""
  id: String!
  """The initial amount of `token` added to the pair."""
  initialPoolAmount: String!
  """The name of the token."""
  name: String!
  """The network ID the token is deployed on."""
  networkId: Int!
  """The ID of the pair (`pairAddress:networkId`)."""
  pairId: String!
  """The percent change `token` remaining in the pair since the initial add."""

  """The symbol for the token."""
```

## LatestToken

Metadata for a newly created token.

<ResponseField name="id" type="String!" required>
  The id of the new token. (tokenAddress:networkId)
</ResponseField>

  The contract address of the new token.
</ResponseField>

  The network ID the token is deployed on.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="blockNumber" type="Int!" required>
  The block number of the token contract's creation.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="transactionIndex" type="Int!" required>
  The index of the transaction within the block.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="traceIndex" type="Int!" required>

</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="transactionHash" type="String!" required>
  The unique hash for the token contract's creation transaction.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="blockHash" type="String!" required>
  The unique hash for the token contract's creation block.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="timeCreated" type="Int!" required>

</ResponseField>

  The address of the token creator.
</ResponseField>

</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="tokenName" type="String!" required>
  The name of the token.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="totalSupply" type="String!" required>
  The total supply of the token.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="tokenSymbol" type="String!" required>
  The symbol of the token.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="decimals" type="Int!" required>
  The token's number of decimals.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="simulationResults" type="[LatestTokenSimResults!]!" required>
  Simulated token contract results, if available.
</ResponseField>

```graphql 
"""Metadata for a newly created token."""
type LatestToken {
  """The id of the new token. (tokenAddress:networkId)"""
  id: String!
  """The contract address of the new token."""
  tokenAddress: String!
  """The network ID the token is deployed on."""
  networkId: Int!
  """The block number of the token contract's creation."""
  blockNumber: Int!
  """The index of the transaction within the block."""
  transactionIndex: Int!
  """The index of the trace within the token contract's creation transaction."""
  traceIndex: Int!
  """The unique hash for the token contract's creation transaction."""
  transactionHash: String!
  """The unique hash for the token contract's creation block."""
  blockHash: String!
  """The unix timestamp for the creation of the token."""
  timeCreated: Int!
  """The address of the token creator."""
  creatorAddress: String!
  """The token creator's network token balance."""
  creatorBalance: String!
  """The name of the token."""
  tokenName: String!
  """The total supply of the token."""
  totalSupply: String!
  """The symbol of the token."""
  tokenSymbol: String!
  """The token's number of decimals."""
  decimals: Int!
  """Simulated token contract results, if available."""

}
```

## LatestTokenSimResults

Metadata for a newly created token.

<ResponseField name="buySuccess" type="Boolean">
  Whether or not a token was able to be succesfully bought during simulation.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="buyTax" type="String">
  Tax paid for a buy transaction during simulation.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="buyGasUsed" type="String">
  Gas used for a buy transaction during simulation.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="maxBuyAmount" type="String">
  The maximum token amount an address can buy during simulation.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="sellSuccess" type="Boolean">
  Whether or not a token was able to be succesfully sold during simulation.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="sellTax" type="String">
  Tax paid for a sell transaction during simulation.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="sellGasUsed" type="String">
  Gas used for a sell transaction during simulation.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="maxSellAmount" type="String">
  The maximum token amount an address can sell during simulation.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="canTransferOwnership" type="Boolean">
  Whether or not the contract ownership was able to be transferred during simulation.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="canRenounceOwnership" type="Boolean">
  Whether or not the contract ownership was able to be renounced during simulation.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="isOwnerRenounced" type="Boolean">
  Whether or not the contract ownership is already renounced during simulation (owner is 0x0).
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="openTradingCall" type="String">
  If a call was found to trigger liquidity & trading, this is the call name.
</ResponseField>

```graphql 
"""Metadata for a newly created token."""
type LatestTokenSimResults {
  """Whether or not a token was able to be succesfully bought during simulation."""
  buySuccess: Boolean
  """Tax paid for a buy transaction during simulation."""
  buyTax: String
  """Gas used for a buy transaction during simulation."""
  buyGasUsed: String
  """The maximum token amount an address can buy during simulation."""
  maxBuyAmount: String
  """Whether or not a token was able to be succesfully sold during simulation."""
  sellSuccess: Boolean
  """Tax paid for a sell transaction during simulation."""
  sellTax: String
  """Gas used for a sell transaction during simulation."""
  sellGasUsed: String
  """The maximum token amount an address can sell during simulation."""
  maxSellAmount: String
  """Whether or not the contract ownership was able to be transferred during simulation."""
  canTransferOwnership: Boolean
  """Whether or not the contract ownership was able to be renounced during simulation."""
  canRenounceOwnership: Boolean
  """Whether or not the contract ownership is already renounced during simulation (owner is 0x0)."""
  isOwnerRenounced: Boolean
  """If a call was found to trigger liquidity & trading, this is the call name."""
  openTradingCall: String
}
```

```graphql 
  """Indicates if the launchpad is completed."""

  """The slot number when the launchpad was completed."""
  completedSlot: Int
  """The slot number when the launchpad was migrated."""
  migratedSlot: Int
  """The unix timestamp when the launchpad was migrated."""
  migratedAt: Int
```

## LiquidityLock

A record of locked liquidity.

<ResponseField name="pairAddress" type="String!" required>
  The pair address.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="networkId" type="Int!" required>
  The network ID the pair is deployed on.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="ownerAddress" type="String!" required>
  The wallet address of the owner.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="lockerAddress" type="String!" required>
  The address of the locker contract.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="createdAt" type="Int!" required>
  The unix timestamp for when the lock was created.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="unlockAt" type="Int">
  The unix timestamp for when the lock expires.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="lockProtocol" type="LiquidityLockProtocol!" required>
  The protocol with which the liquidity is locked.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="liquidityProtocol" type="LiquidityProtocol!" required>
  The protocol that created the pair
  
  <Warning>
    This field is deprecated. Use liquidityProtocolV2 instead
  </Warning>
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="liquidityProtocolV2" type="String!" required>
  The protocol that created the pair
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="liquidityAmount" type="String!" required>
  The amount of liquidity locked.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="initialAmountToken0" type="String!" required>
  The inital amount of token0 locked.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="initialAmountToken1" type="String!" required>
  The inital amount of token1 locked.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="liquidityNftData" type="LiquidityNftData">
  If the liquidity position is represented by an NFT, this will contain the NFT data.
</ResponseField>

```graphql 
"""A record of locked liquidity."""
type LiquidityLock {
  """The pair address."""
  pairAddress: String!
  """The network ID the pair is deployed on."""
  networkId: Int!
  """The wallet address of the owner."""
  ownerAddress: String!
  """The address of the locker contract."""
  lockerAddress: String!
  """The unix timestamp for when the lock was created."""
  createdAt: Int!
  """The unix timestamp for when the lock expires."""
  unlockAt: Int
  """The protocol with which the liquidity is locked."""
  lockProtocol: LiquidityLockProtocol!
  """The protocol that created the pair"""
  liquidityProtocol: LiquidityProtocol! @deprecated(reason: "Use liquidityProtocolV2 instead")
  """The protocol that created the pair"""
  liquidityProtocolV2: String!
  """The amount of liquidity locked."""
  liquidityAmount: String!
  """The inital amount of token0 locked."""
  initialAmountToken0: String!
  """The inital amount of token1 locked."""
  initialAmountToken1: String!
  """If the liquidity position is represented by an NFT, this will contain the NFT data."""
  liquidityNftData: LiquidityNftData
}
```

```graphql 
  """The locked amount of tokens in pairs."""

  """The locked amount of tokens in pairs shifted by number of decimals the token has."""
```

## MarketCapEventWebhookCondition

Webhook conditions for a market cap event.

<ResponseField name="tokenAddress" type="StringEqualsCondition!" required>
  The token contract address the webhook is listening for.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="networkId" type="IntEqualsCondition!" required>
  The network ID the webhook is listening on.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="fdvMarketCapUsd" type="ComparisonOperator">
  The market cap condition that must be met in order for the webhook to send.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="circulatingMarketCapUsd" type="ComparisonOperator">
  The circulating market cap condition that must be met in order for the webhook to send.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="pairAddress" type="StringEqualsCondition">
  The pair contract address the webhook is listening for.
</ResponseField>

```graphql 
"""Webhook conditions for a market cap event."""
type MarketCapEventWebhookCondition {
  """The token contract address the webhook is listening for."""
  tokenAddress: StringEqualsCondition!
  """The network ID the webhook is listening on."""
  networkId: IntEqualsCondition!
  """The market cap condition that must be met in order for the webhook to send."""
  fdvMarketCapUsd: ComparisonOperator
  """The circulating market cap condition that must be met in order for the webhook to send."""
  circulatingMarketCapUsd: ComparisonOperator
  """The pair contract address the webhook is listening for."""
  pairAddress: StringEqualsCondition
}
```

## MetadataResponse

The status for a network supported on Defined.

<ResponseField name="lastProcessedBlock" type="Int">
  The last processed block on the network.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="lastProcessedTimestamp" type="Int">
  The unix timestamp for the last processed block on the network.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="networkId" type="Int!" required>
  The network ID.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="networkName" type="String!" required>
  The name of the network.
</ResponseField>

```graphql 
"""The status for a network supported on Defined."""
type MetadataResponse {
  """The last processed block on the network."""
  lastProcessedBlock: Int
  """The unix timestamp for the last processed block on the network."""
  lastProcessedTimestamp: Int
  """The network ID."""
  networkId: Int!
  """The name of the network."""
  networkName: String!
}
```

---

## MintEventData

Event data for a token mint event.

<ResponseField name="amount0" type="String">
  The amount of `token0` added to the pair.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="amount1" type="String">
  The amount of `token1` added to the pair.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="amount0Shifted" type="String">
  The amount of `token0` added to the pair, adjusted by the number of decimals in the token. For example, if `amount0` is in WEI, `amount0Shifted` will be in ETH.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="amount1Shifted" type="String">
  The amount of `token1` added to the pair, adjusted by the number of decimals in the token. For example, USDC `amount1Shifted` will be by 6 decimals.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="tickLower" type="String">
  The lower tick boundary of the position. Only applicable for UniswapV3 events.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="tickUpper" type="String">
  The upper tick boundary of the position. Only applicable for UniswapV3 events.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="type" type="EventType!" required>
  The type of token event, `Mint`.
</ResponseField>

```graphql 
"""Event data for a token mint event."""
type MintEventData {
  """The amount of `token0` added to the pair."""
  amount0: String
  """The amount of `token1` added to the pair."""
  amount1: String
  """The amount of `token0` added to the pair, adjusted by the number of decimals in the token. For example, if `amount0` is in WEI, `amount0Shifted` will be in ETH."""
  amount0Shifted: String
  """The amount of `token1` added to the pair, adjusted by the number of decimals in the token. For example, USDC `amount1Shifted` will be by 6 decimals."""
  amount1Shifted: String
  """The lower tick boundary of the position. Only applicable for UniswapV3 events."""
  tickLower: String
  """The upper tick boundary of the position. Only applicable for UniswapV3 events."""
  tickUpper: String
  """The type of token event, `Mint`."""
  type: EventType!
}
```

## Network

A network supported on Defined.

<ResponseField name="name" type="String!" required>
  The name of the network. For example, `arbitrum`.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="id" type="Int!" required>
  The network ID. For example, `42161` for `arbitrum`.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="networkShortName" type="String">
  No description provided
</ResponseField>

```graphql 
"""A network supported on Defined."""
type Network {
  """The name of the network. For example, `arbitrum`."""
  name: String!
  """The network ID. For example, `42161` for `arbitrum`."""
  id: Int!
  networkShortName: String
}
```

</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="statsWeek1" type="WindowedWalletStats">
  The stats for the last week
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="statsDay30" type="WindowedWalletStats">
  The stats for the last 30 days
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="statsYear1" type="WindowedWalletStats">
  The stats for the last year
</ResponseField>

```graphql

type NetworkBreakdown {
  """The network ID"""
  networkId: Int!
  """The native token balance"""
  nativeTokenBalance: String!
  """The stats for the last day"""
  statsDay1: WindowedWalletStats
  """The stats for the last week"""
  statsWeek1: WindowedWalletStats
  """The stats for the last 30 days"""
  statsDay30: WindowedWalletStats
  """The stats for the last year"""
  statsYear1: WindowedWalletStats
}
```

## NetworkWalletFilterConnection

A connection of wallets matching a filter on a specific network.

<ResponseField name="results" type="[NetworkWalletFilterResult!]!" required>
  The list of wallets matching the filter parameters.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="count" type="Int!" required>
  The number of wallets returned.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="offset" type="Int!" required>
  Where in the list the server started when returning items.
</ResponseField>

```graphql 
"""A connection of wallets matching a filter on a specific network."""
type NetworkWalletFilterConnection {
  """The list of wallets matching the filter parameters."""
  results: [NetworkWalletFilterResult!]!
  """The number of wallets returned."""
  count: Int!
  """Where in the list the server started when returning items."""
  offset: Int!
}
```

## NewPoolEventData

Event data for creating a new NFT pool.

<ResponseField name="type" type="NftPoolEventType!" required>
  The type of NFT pool event, `NEW_POOL`.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="networkId" type="Int!" required>
  The network ID the NFT collection is deployed on.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="poolAddress" type="String!" required>
  The contract address of the NFT pool.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="collectionAddress" type="String!" required>
  The contract address of the NFT collection.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="tokenAddress" type="String!" required>
  The contract address of the liquidity token of the pool (usually WETH).
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="ownerAddress" type="String!" required>
  The wallet address of the pool owner.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="assetRecipientAddress" type="String!" required>
  The wallet address that will receive the tokens or NFT sent to the pair during swaps.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="bondingCurveAddress" type="String!" required>
  The contract address of the bonding curve.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="bondingCurveType" type="BondingCurveType!" required>
  The bonding curve type that defines how the prices of NFTs change after each buy or sell within a pool.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="delta" type="String!" required>
  The initial delta used in the bonding curve.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="feeAmountT" type="String!" required>
  The pool fee amount in the pool's liquidity token.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="startPriceT" type="String!" required>
  The initial spot price in the pool's liquidity token.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="buyPriceT" type="String!" required>
  The initial price at which the pool is willing to buy an NFT in the pool's liquidity token.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="sellPriceT" type="String!" required>
  The initial price at which the pool is willing to sell an NFT in the pool's liquidity token.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="createdAt" type="Int!" required>
  The unix timestamp for the time the pool was created.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="nftTokenBalance" type="String!" required>
  The number of NFTs in the contract after the block has processed.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="tokenBalanceT" type="String!" required>
  The amount of token in the contract after the block has processed in the pool's liquidity token.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="nbtRatio" type="String!" required>
  The ratio of the transaction token to the network's base token.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="usdRatio" type="String!" required>
  The ratio of the transaction token to USD.
</ResponseField>

```graphql 
"""Event data for creating a new NFT pool."""
type NewPoolEventData {
  """The type of NFT pool event, `NEW_POOL`."""
  type: NftPoolEventType!
  """The network ID the NFT collection is deployed on."""
  networkId: Int!
  """The contract address of the NFT pool."""
  poolAddress: String!
  """The contract address of the NFT collection."""
  collectionAddress: String!
  """The contract address of the liquidity token of the pool (usually WETH)."""
  tokenAddress: String!
  """The wallet address of the pool owner."""
  ownerAddress: String!
  """The wallet address that will receive the tokens or NFT sent to the pair during swaps."""
  assetRecipientAddress: String!
  """The contract address of the bonding curve."""
  bondingCurveAddress: String!
  """The bonding curve type that defines how the prices of NFTs change after each buy or sell within a pool."""
  bondingCurveType: BondingCurveType!
  """The initial delta used in the bonding curve."""
  delta: String!
  """The pool fee amount in the pool's liquidity token."""
  feeAmountT: String!
  """The initial spot price in the pool's liquidity token."""
  startPriceT: String!
  """The initial price at which the pool is willing to buy an NFT in the pool's liquidity token."""
  buyPriceT: String!
  """The initial price at which the pool is willing to sell an NFT in the pool's liquidity token."""
  sellPriceT: String!
  """The unix timestamp for the time the pool was created."""
  createdAt: Int!
  """The number of NFTs in the contract after the block has processed."""
  nftTokenBalance: String!
  """The amount of token in the contract after the block has processed in the pool's liquidity token."""
  tokenBalanceT: String!
  """The ratio of the transaction token to the network's base token."""
  nbtRatio: String!
  """The ratio of the transaction token to USD."""
  usdRatio: String!
}
```

<ResponseField name="feeAmountT" type="String!" required>

<ResponseField name="startPriceT" type="String!" required>

</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="createdAt" type="Int!" required>

</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="tokenBalanceT" type="String!" required>
  The amount of token in the contract after the block has processed in the pool's liquidity token.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="nbtRatio" type="String!" required>
  The ratio of the transaction token to the network's base token.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="usdRatio" type="String!" required>
  The ratio of the transaction token to USD.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="nftTokenIds" type="[String!]!" required>
  The list of NFT token IDs initially deposited.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="nftTokenQuantities" type="[String]!" required>
  The amount of each NFT token initially deposited.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="nftAssets" type="[NftAsset]">
  *New Param*: The list of NFT assets withdrawn. More extensive info than nftTokenIds.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="poolNftType" type="PoolNftType!" required>
  The type of NFT in the pool.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="royalties" type="[NftPoolRoyalty]">
  The list of royalties for the pool. Only applicable for `SUDOSWAP_V2` pools.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="propertyChecker" type="String">
  The property checker contract address for the pool.
</ResponseField>

```graphql 
"""Event data for creating a new NFT pool."""
type NewPoolEventDataV2 {
  """The type of NFT pool event, `NEW_POOL`."""
  type: NftPoolEventType!
  """The network ID the NFT collection is deployed on."""
  networkId: Int!
  """The contract address of the NFT pool."""
  poolAddress: String!
  """The contract address of the NFT collection."""
  collectionAddress: String!
  """The contract address of the liquidity token of the pool (usually WETH)."""
  tokenAddress: String!
  """The wallet address of the pool owner."""
  ownerAddress: String!
  """The wallet address that will receive the tokens or NFT sent to the pair during swaps."""
  assetRecipientAddress: String!
  """The contract address of the bonding curve."""
  bondingCurveAddress: String!
  """The bonding curve type that defines how the prices of NFTs change after each buy or sell within a pool."""
  bondingCurveType: BondingCurveType!
  """The initial delta used in the bonding curve."""
  delta: String!
  """The pool fee amount in the pool's liquidity token."""
  feeAmountT: String!
  """The initial spot price in the pool's liquidity token."""
  startPriceT: String!
  """The initial price at which the pool is willing to buy an NFT in the pool's liquidity token."""
  buyPriceT: String!
  """The initial price at which the pool is willing to sell an NFT in the pool's liquidity token."""
  sellPriceT: String!
  """The unix timestamp for the time the pool was created."""
  createdAt: Int!
  """The amount of token in the contract after the block has processed in the pool's liquidity token."""
  tokenBalanceT: String!
  """The ratio of the transaction token to the network's base token."""
  nbtRatio: String!
  """The ratio of the transaction token to USD."""
  usdRatio: String!
  """The list of NFT token IDs initially deposited."""
  nftTokenIds: [String!]!
  """The amount of each NFT token initially deposited."""
  nftTokenQuantities: [String]!
  """*New Param*: The list of NFT assets withdrawn. More extensive info than nftTokenIds."""
  nftAssets: [NftAsset]
  """The type of NFT in the pool."""
  poolNftType: PoolNftType!
  """The list of royalties for the pool. Only applicable for `SUDOSWAP_V2` pools."""
  royalties: [NftPoolRoyalty]
  """The property checker contract address for the pool."""
  propertyChecker: String
}
```

## NftAsset

An NFT asset.

<ResponseField name="id" type="String!" required>
  The ID of the NFT asset (`address`:`networkId`).
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="address" type="String!" required>

</ResponseField>

```graphql 
  """The name of the NFT asset."""

  """The description of the NFT asset."""

  """The source image URI linked by smart contract metadata."""
  originalImage: String
  """The URI provided by the smart contract. Typically JSON that contains metadata."""
  uri: String
  """The attributes for the NFT asset."""
  attributes: [NftAssetAttribute!]
  """The number of NFT assets with the same NFT token ID. Only applicable for ERC1155 tokens."""

  """Raw NFT metadata from the smart contract."""
```

## NftAssetAttribute

Attributes for an NFT asset.

<ResponseField name="class" type="String">

</ResponseField>

  The attribute display type. Can be `Trait`, `Stat`, `Ranking`, `BoostNumber`, `BoostPercentage` or `Date`.
</ResponseField>

  The max value, if applicable.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="name" type="String!" required>
  The name of the attribute.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="value" type="String!" required>
  The value of the attribute.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="valueType" type="NftAssetAttributeType!" required>
  The type for the `value` field. Can be `String`, `Number` or `Array`.
</ResponseField>

```graphql

type NftAssetAttribute {

  class: String
  """Suggested CSS styling. An optional attribute of ERC-1155 assets."""
  css: String
  """The attribute display type. Can be `Trait`, `Stat`, `Ranking`, `BoostNumber`, `BoostPercentage` or `Date`."""
  displayType: NftAssetAttributeDisplayType!
  """The max value, if applicable."""
  maxValue: String
  """The name of the attribute."""
  name: String!
  """The value of the attribute."""
  value: String!
  """The type for the `value` field. Can be `String`, `Number` or `Array`."""
  valueType: NftAssetAttributeType!
}
```

## NftCollectionFilterResult

An NFT collection matching a set of filter parameters.

<ResponseField name="id" type="String">
  The ID of the NFT collection (`address`:`networkId`).
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="address" type="String">
  The contract address of the NFT collection.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="grouping" type="String">
  The marketplace address or `all`. Can be used to get marketplace-specific metrics.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="networkId" type="Int">
  The network ID the NFT collection is deployed on.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="name" type="String">
  The name of the NFT collection.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="symbol" type="String">
  The symbol of the NFT collection.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="lastEventTimestamp" type="Int">
  The unix timestamp for the last event.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="ercType" type="String">
  The token standard. Can be a variation of `ERC-721` or `ERC-1155`.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="imageUrl" type="String">
  The image URL for the collection or one of the assets within the collection.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="totalSupply" type="String">
  The total supply of the NFT collection.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="timestamp" type="Int">
  The unix timestamp indicating the last time the data was updated. Updates daily.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="stats1h" type="NftStatsWindowWithChange">
  Stats for the past hour.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="stats4h" type="NftStatsWindowWithChange">
  Stats for the past 4 hours.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="stats12h" type="NftStatsWindowWithChange">
  Stats for the past 12 hours.
</ResponseField>

<ResponseField name="stats24h" type="NftStatsWindowWithChange">
  Stats for the past 24 hours.
</ResponseField>

```graphql 
"""An NFT collection matching a set of filter parameters."""
type NftCollectionFilterResult {
  """The ID of the NFT collection (`address`:`networkId`)."""
  id: String
  """The contract address of the NFT collection."""
  address: String
  """The marketplace address or `all`. Can be used to get marketplace-specific metrics."""
  grouping: String
  """The network ID the NFT collection is deployed on."""
  networkId: Int
  """The name of the NFT collection."""
  name: String
  """The symbol of the NFT collection."""
  symbol: String
  """The unix timestamp for the last event."""
  lastEventTimestamp: Int
  """The token standard. Can be a variation of `ERC-721` or `ERC-1155`."""
  ercType: String
  """The image URL for the collection or one of the assets within the collection."""
  imageUrl: String
  """The total supply of the NFT collection."""
  totalSupply: String
  """The unix timestamp indicating the last time the data was updated. Updates daily."""
  timestamp: Int
  """Stats for the past hour."""
  stats1h: NftStatsWindowWithChange
  """Stats for the past 4 hours."""
  stats4h: NftStatsWindowWithChange
  """Stats for the past 12 hours."""
  stats12h: NftStatsWindowWithChange
  """Stats for the past 24 hours."""
  stats24h: NftStatsWindowWithChange
}
```
